\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Helper\ for\ computeProductBlockingSizes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Given\ a\ m\ x\ k\ times\ k\ x\ n\ matrix\ product\ of\ scalar\ types\ \(\backslash\)c\ LhsScalar\ and\ \(\backslash\)c\ RhsScalar,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ this\ function\ computes\ the\ blocking\ size\ parameters\ along\ the\ respective\ dimensions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ for\ matrix\ products\ and\ related\ algorithms.\ The\ blocking\ sizes\ depends\ on\ various}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ the\ L1\ and\ L2\ cache\ sizes,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ the\ register\ level\ blocking\ sizes\ defined\ by\ gebp\_traits,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ the\ number\ of\ scalars\ that\ fit\ into\ a\ packet\ (when\ vectorization\ is\ enabled).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \(\backslash\)sa\ setCpuCacheSizes\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ LhsScalar,\ \textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ RhsScalar,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ KcFactor,\ \textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ Index>}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ evaluateProductBlockingSizesHeuristic(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}\&\ k,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}\&\ m,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}\&\ n,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}\ num\_threads\ =\ 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ gebp\_traits<LhsScalar,RhsScalar>\ Traits;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Explanations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Let's\ recall\ that\ the\ product\ algorithms\ form\ mc\ x\ kc\ vertical\ panels\ A'\ on\ the\ lhs\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ kc\ x\ nc\ blocks\ B'\ on\ the\ rhs.\ B'\ has\ to\ fit\ into\ L2/L3\ cache.\ Moreover,\ A'\ is\ processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ per\ mr\ x\ kc\ horizontal\ small\ panels\ where\ mr\ is\ the\ blocking\ size\ along\ the\ m\ dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ at\ the\ register\ level.\ This\ small\ horizontal\ panel\ has\ to\ stay\ within\ L1\ cache.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \ \ std::ptrdiff\_t\ l1,\ l2,\ l3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \ \ manage\_caching\_sizes(GetAction,\ \&l1,\ \&l2,\ \&l3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00135\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \#ifdef\ EIGEN\_VECTORIZE\_AVX512}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00136\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ need\ to\ find\ a\ rationale\ for\ that,\ but\ without\ this\ adjustment,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ performance\ with\ AVX512\ is\ pretty\ bad,\ like\ -\/20\%\ slower.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00138\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ One\ reason\ is\ that\ with\ increasing\ packet-\/size,\ the\ blocking\ size\ k}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00139\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ has\ to\ become\ pretty\ small\ if\ we\ want\ that\ 1\ lhs\ panel\ fit\ within\ L1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ For\ instance,\ with\ the\ 3pX4\ kernel\ and\ double,\ the\ size\ of\ the\ lhs+rhs\ panels\ are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ k*(3*64\ +\ 4*8)\ Bytes,\ with\ l1=32kBytes,\ and\ k\%8=0,\ we\ have\ k=144.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ is\ quite\ small\ for\ a\ good\ reuse\ of\ the\ accumulation\ registers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \ \ l1\ *=\ 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00206\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00207\ \ \ \ \ \ \ k\_peeling\ =\ 8,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00208\ \ \ \ \ \ \ k\_div\ =\ KcFactor\ *\ (Traits::mr\ *\ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(LhsScalar)\ +\ Traits::nr\ *\ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(RhsScalar)),}
\DoxyCodeLine{00209\ \ \ \ \ \ \ k\_sub\ =\ Traits::mr\ *\ Traits::nr\ *\ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(ResScalar)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00210\ \ \ \ \ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00211\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00212\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/-\/-\/-\/\ 1st\ level\ of\ blocking\ on\ L1,\ yields\ kc\ -\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00213\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Blocking\ on\ the\ third\ dimension\ (i.e.,\ k)\ is\ chosen\ so\ that\ an\ horizontal\ panel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00215\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ size\ mr\ x\ kc\ of\ the\ lhs\ plus\ a\ vertical\ panel\ of\ kc\ x\ nr\ of\ the\ rhs\ both\ fits\ within\ L1\ cache.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00216\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ also\ include\ a\ register-\/level\ block\ of\ the\ result\ (mx\ x\ nr).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00217\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (In\ an\ ideal\ world\ only\ the\ lhs\ panel\ would\ stay\ in\ L1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00218\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Moreover,\ kc\ has\ to\ be\ a\ multiple\ of\ 8\ to\ be\ compatible\ with\ loop\ peeling,\ leading\ to\ a\ maximum\ blocking\ size\ of:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00219\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}\ max\_kc\ =\ numext::maxi<Index>(((l1-\/k\_sub)/k\_div)\ \&\ (\string~(k\_peeling-\/1)),1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00220\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}\ old\_k\ =\ k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00221\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(k>max\_kc)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00222\ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00223\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ are\ really\ blocking\ on\ the\ third\ dimension:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00224\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/>\ reduce\ blocking\ size\ to\ make\ sure\ the\ last\ block\ is\ as\ large\ as\ possible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00225\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ while\ keeping\ the\ same\ number\ of\ sweeps\ over\ the\ result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00226\ \ \ \ \ \ \ k\ =\ (k\%max\_kc)==0\ ?\ max\_kc}
\DoxyCodeLine{00227\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ :\ max\_kc\ -\/\ k\_peeling\ *\ ((max\_kc-\/1-\/(k\%max\_kc))/(k\_peeling*(k/max\_kc+1)));}

\DoxyCodeLine{00234\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TODO\ find\ a\ reliable\ way\ to\ get\ the\ actual\ amount\ of\ cache\ per\ core\ to\ use\ for\ 2nd\ level\ blocking,\ that\ is:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00236\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ number\ below\ is\ quite\ conservative:\ it\ is\ better\ to\ underestimate\ the\ cache\ size\ rather\ than\ overestimating\ it)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00237\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ For\ instance,\ it\ corresponds\ to\ 6MB\ of\ L3\ shared\ among\ 4\ cores.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00242\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00243\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00244\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Here,\ nc\ is\ chosen\ such\ that\ a\ block\ of\ kc\ x\ nc\ of\ the\ rhs\ fit\ within\ half\ of\ L2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00245\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ second\ half\ is\ implicitly\ reserved\ to\ access\ the\ result\ and\ lhs\ coefficients.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00246\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ When\ k<max\_kc,\ then\ nc\ can\ arbitrarily\ growth.\ In\ practice,\ it\ seems\ to\ be\ fruitful}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00247\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ limit\ this\ growth:\ we\ bound\ nc\ to\ growth\ by\ a\ factor\ x1.5.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00248\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ However,\ if\ the\ entire\ lhs\ block\ fit\ within\ L1,\ then\ we\ are\ not\ going\ to\ block\ on\ the\ rows\ at\ all,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00249\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ it\ becomes\ fruitful\ to\ keep\ the\ packed\ rhs\ blocks\ in\ L1\ if\ there\ is\ enough\ remaining\ space.}}
